_Thinking:_

Good. Now I know that `generarOpl` and `generarOplInteractivo` are imported in the PanelOpl.tsx component and in tests. The store doesn't need to import them - the PanelOpl component calls them directly. For the `copiarOplActualAlPortapapeles` and `exportarOplActualHtml` actions, I need the OPL text to copy/export. But the store doesn't have access to `generarOplInteractivo`. 

Looking at the brief, the store actions should:
- `copiarOplActualAlPortapapeles`: needs OPL text → I can either import `generarOpl` in the store or pass the text from the component
- `exportarOplActualHtml`: needs HTML strings

Actually, the brief says: "copiarOplActualAlPortapapeles usa navigator.clipboard.writeText(opl)". And the store can access `modelo` and `opdActivoId`. So I can import `generarOpl` (the non-interactive version) in the store to get the plain text, and generate HTML manually.

But the brief also says: "No introducir libreria de export HTML; usar generacion manual de string + Blob + <a download> con DOM nativo."

Let me import `generarOpl` in store.ts and implement the actions.

Wait, looking at the brief more carefully: "fijarBusquedaOpl solo actualiza estado UI." and "copiarOplActualAlPortapapeles usa navigator.clipboard.writeText(opl)." So the store needs the OPL text for copy/export. Let me import `generarOpl` from the OPL module.

2218:   return { ...indice, modelos, recientes: indice.recientes.filter((r) => idsGuardados.has(r)) };
2219: }
2220: 
2221: function esRecord(value: unknown): value is Record<string, unknown> {
2222:   return typeof value === "object" && value !== null && !Array.isArray(value);
2223: }
2224: 
2225: function modelosRecientesDeIndice(indice: WorkspaceIndice, guardados: ResumenModeloPersistido[]): ResumenModeloPersistido[] {
2226:   return indice.recientes
2227:     .map((id) => guardados.find((m) => m.id === id))
2228:     .filter((m): m is ResumenModeloPersistido => m !== undefined);
2229: }

(End of file - total 2229 lines)
</content>
```

```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/felix/projects/deep-opm-pro/app/src/store.ts",
  "newString": "function modelosRecientesDeIndice(indice: WorkspaceIndice, guardados: ResumenModeloPersistido[]): ResumenModeloPersistido[] {\n  return indice.recientes\n    .map((id) => guardados.find((m) => m.id === id))\n    .filter((m): m is ResumenModeloPersistido => m !== undefined);\n}\n\n/**\n * HU-50.024: Genera HTML autocontenido con estilos canónicos OPL-ES (JOYAS §1).\n * Colores: objeto #70E483, proceso #3BC3FF, estado #586D8C.\n */\nfunction generarHtmlOpl(lineas: string[], titulo: string): string {\n  const escapeHtml = (texto: string) =>\n    texto\n      .replace(/&/g, \"&amp;\")\n      .replace(/</g, \"&lt;\")\n      .replace(/>/g, \"&gt;\")\n      .replace(/\"/g, \"&quot;\");\n\n  const filas = lineas\n    .map((linea, i) => {\n      // Colorear tokens markdown: **objeto** y *proceso*\n      const coloreada = linea\n        .replace(/\\*\\*([^*]+)\\*\\*/g, '<span class=\"obj\">$1</span>')\n        .replace(/\\*([^*\\s][^*]*?)\\*/g, '<span class=\"proc\">$1</span>')\n        .replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<span class=\"est\">$1</span>');\n      return `<tr><td class=\"num\">${i + 1}.</td><td>${coloreada}</td></tr>`;\n    })\n    .join(\"\\n\");\n\n  return `<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html lang=\"es\">\n<head>\n<meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n<title>OPL-ES — ${escapeHtml(titulo)}</title>\n<style>\n  body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 1.65; color: #1f2937; max-width: 960px; margin: 40px auto; padding: 0 20px; }\n  h1 { font-size: 18px; color: #334155; margin-bottom: 24px; }\n  table { border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; }\n  td { vertical-align: top; padding: 2px 6px; }\n  td.num { color: #667085; text-align: right; width: 32px; font-variant-numeric: tabular-nums; }\n  .obj { color: #1f7a3c; font-weight: 700; }\n  .proc { color: #147aa5; font-style: italic; font-weight: 700; }\n  .est { color: #475467; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, Menlo, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 12px; }\n</style>\n</head>\n<body>\n<h1>OPL-ES &mdash; ${escapeHtml(titulo)}</h1>\n<table>${filas}</table>\n</body>\n</html>`;\n}",
  "oldString": "function modelosRecientesDeIndice(indice: WorkspaceIndice, guardados: ResumenModeloPersistido[]): ResumenModeloPersistido[] {\n  return indice.recientes\n    .map((id) => guardados.find((m) => m.id === id))\n    .filter((m): m is ResumenModeloPersistido => m !== undefined);\n}"

setEdicion: (value: { tipo: \"entidad\" | \"estado\"; id: string; tokenId: string; valor: string } | null) => void;\n  seleccionarDesdeOpl: (ref: OplReferencia) => void;\n  renombrarEntidadDesdeOpl: autoFocus\n        style={style.inputInline}\n        onInput={(event) =>\n          setEdicion({\n            ...edicion,\n            valor: (event.currentTarget as HTMLInputElement).value,\n          })\n        }\n        onKeyDown={(event) => {\n          if (event.key === \"Enter\") {\n            renombrarEntidadDesdeOpl(edicion.id, edicion.valor);\n            setEdicion(null);\n          }\n          if (event.key === \"Escape\") setEdicion(null);\n        }}\n        onBlur={() => setEdicion(null)}\n      />\n    );\n  }\n\n  // ── Edición inline para estado ──\n  if (token.ref?.tipo     autoFocus\n        style={style.inputInline}\n        onInput={(event) =>\n          setEdicion({\n            ...edicion,\n            valor: (event.currentTarget as HTMLInputElement).value,\n ...(seleccionado ? style.tokenHover : {}),\n      ...styleTokenMarkdown(token),\n      // Señal visual para tokens multi-enlace (HU-50.021): subrayado punteado\n      ...(isEnlaceDestino ? (token.ref) {\n        seleccionarDesdeOpl(token.ref);\n      }\n    },\n    onDblClick: () => {\n      if (token.ref?.tipo === \"entidad\") {\n        setEdicion({\n          tipo: \"entidad\",\n tipo: \"estado\",\n          id: token.ref.id,\n          tokenId: token.id,\n          valor: token.texto.replace(/`/g, \"\"),\n        });\n        return;\n      }\n      // Doble clic en verbo → seleccionar y abrir inspector (HU-50.022)\n      if (token.rol === \"verbo\" && enlaceRef) {\n        abrirInspectorEnlaceDesdeOpl(enlaceRef.id);\n        return;\n      }\n      if (token.ref?.tipo === \"enlace\") {\n        abrirInspectorEnlaceDesdeOpl(token.ref.id);\n      }\n    },\n  };\n\n  if (token.markdown === \"objeto\")\n    return <strong {...common}>{contenido}</strong>;\n  if (token.markdown === \"proceso\")\n    return <em {...common}>{contenido}</em>;\n  if (token.markdown === \"estado\")\n    return <code {...common}>{token.texto}</code>;\n  return <span {...common}>{token.texto}</span>;\n}\n\n// ── Helpers ──\n\nfunction textoVisibleToken(token: OplToken): string {\n  if (token.markdown === \"objeto\") {\n    return token.texto.replace(/\\*\\*([^*]+)\\*\\*/g, \"$1\");\n  }\n  if (token.markdown === \"proceso\") {\n    return token.texto.replace(/\\*([^*\\s][^*]*?)\\*/g, \"$1\");\n  }\n  // Quitar backticks para estados\n  return token.texto.replace(/`/g, \"\");\n}\n\nfunction styleTokenMarkdown(token: OplToken): preact.JSX.CSSProperties {\n  if (token.markdown === \"objeto\") return style.objeto;\n  if (token.markdown === \"proceso\") return style.proceso;\n  if (token.markdown === \"estado\") return style.estado;\n  if (token.rol === \"verbo\") return style.verbo;\n  return {};\n}\n\n// ── Estilos ──\n\nconst style = {\n  panel: {\n    overflow: \"auto\",\n    padding: \"10px 14px\",\n    background: \"#ffffff\",\n    color: \"#1f2937\",\n    fontSize: \"13px\",\n    lineHeight: 1.65,\n  },\n \"nowrap\",\n  },\n  btnDisabled: {\n    opacity: 0.4,\n    cursor: \"not-allowed\",\n  },\n  toggle: {\n    display: \"inline-flex\",\n    alignItems: \"center\",\n    gap: 4,\n    color: 773:   const id = Object.keys(store.getState().modelo.entidades)[0];
774:   if (!id) throw new Error("La prueba esperaba al menos una entidad");
775:   return id;
776: }
777: 
778: function estadosObjeto(entidadId: string) {
779:   return Object.values(store.getState().modelo.estados)
780:     .filter((estado) => estado.entidadId === entidadId)
781:     .sort((a, b) => a.id.localeCompare(b.id));
782: }
783: 
784: function modeloConOpdHijo(): Modelo {
785:   const modelo = crearModelo();
786:   return {
787:     ...modelo,
788:     opds: {
789:       ...modelo.opds,
790:       "opd-2": {

792:         nombre: "SD1",
793:         padreId: modelo.opdRaizId,
794:         apariencias: {},
795:         enlaces: {},
796:       },
797:     },
798:   };
799: }

801: function modeloConEnlaceDerivado(): {
802:   modelo: Modelo;
803:   opdId: string;
804:   enlaceId: string;
805:   aparienciaEnlaceId: string;
806:   segundoId: string;
807: } {
808:   let modelo = crearModelo("Store derivado");
809:   modelo = must(crearObjeto(modelo, modelo.opdRaizId, { x: 20, y: 100 }, "Entrada"));
810:   modelo = must(crearProceso(modelo, modelo.opdRaizId, { x: 260, y: 120 }, "Procesar"));
811:   const entradaId = entidadPorNombre(modelo, "Entrada");
812:   const procesarId = entidadPorNombre(modelo, "Procesar");
813:   modelo = must(crearEnlace(modelo, modelo.opdRaizId, entradaId, procesarId, "consumo"));
814:   const descompuesto = must(descomponerProceso(modelo, modelo.opdRaizId, procesarId));
815:   modelo = descompuesto.modelo;
816:   const segundoId = entidadPorNombre(modelo, "Procesar 2");
817:   const apariencia = Object.values(modelo.opds[descompuesto.opdId]?.enlaces ?? {})
818:     .find((item) => modelo.enlaces[item.enlaceId]?.tipo === "consumo");
819:   if (!apariencia) throw new Error("La prueba esperaba un enlace consumo derivado");
820:   return {
821:     modelo,
822:     opdId: descompuesto.opdId,
823:     enlaceId: apariencia.enlaceId,
824:     aparienciaEnlaceId: apariencia.id,
825:     segundoId,
826:   };
827: }
828: 
829: function entidadPorNombre(modelo: Modelo, nombre: string): string {
830:   const entidad = Object.values(modelo.entidades).find((item) => item.nombre === nombre);
831:   if (!entidad) throw new Error(`Entidad no encontrada: ${nombre}`);
832:   return entidad.id;
833: }
834: 
835: function must<T>(resultado: { ok: true; value: T } | { ok: false; error: string }): T {
836:   if (!resultado.ok) throw new Error(resultado.error);
837:   return resultado.value;
838: }
839: 
840: function instalarLocalStorage(): void {
841:   const datos = new Map<string, string>();
842:   Object.defineProperty(globalThis, "localStorage", {
843:     configurable: true,
844:     value: {
845:       getItem: (key: string) => datos.get(key) ?? null,
846:       setItem: (key: string, value: string) => datos.set(key, value),
847:       removeItem: (key: string) => datos.delete(key),
848:       clear: () => datos.clear(),
849:     },
850:   });
851: }

OK, let me analyze each failure:

1. **Test #1**: Expected "se despliega en **Motor** y **Rueda**" but got "**Vehiculo** se despliega en **Vehiculo parte 1**, **Vehiculo parte 2**, **Vehiculo parte 3** y **Rueda**." 

This is because `modeloConVehiculoDesplegado()` already creates 3 default parts ("Vehiculo parte 1", "Vehiculo parte 2", "Vehiculo parte 3"). Then I add "Motor" and "Rueda". So the actual sentence includes all 5 parts. I need to either not use `modeloConVehiculoDesplegado` or add my parts to a fresh model.

Let me rewrite the tests to not use `modeloConVehiculoDesplegado` which has 3 default parts.

2. **Test #2**: `lineaEspec!.tokens.find(t => t.rol === "verbo" && t.texto.includes("es un"))` returns undefined. The verb token wasn't generated. This is because the `hintsRefinamiento` with generalizacion mode calls `verboDespliegue` which returns "es un" but the token string might not match exactly. Looking at `oracionDespliegue`: for generalizacion it generates `**Auto** es un **Vehiculo**.` But `verboDespliegue("generalizacion")` returns `"es un"`. The hint text is `"es un"`. But the tokenizer looks for `"es un"` in the sentence. Let me check if `"es un"` exists in the sentence text. Yes, it should. 

Wait, but `hintsRefinamiento` returns the verb hint with an enlace ref. The tokenizer should match it. Let me debug...

Actually, the issue might be simpler. In the generalizacion case, the verb `"es un"` is generated as a hint with `ref: refEnlace(enlaceHijo.id)`. But the tokenizer in `ubicarHint` searches for the exact text. If the hint text is `"es un"` and the sentence is `**Auto** es un **Vehiculo**.`, then `"es un"` should appear as a substring. But maybe the markdown characters are disrupting the tokenization.

Let me look at the tokenizer more carefully. The tokenizer takes all hints, finds their positions, sorts them, and creates tokens. If the hint `"es un"` appears in the text, it should create a token for it. Let me trace through...

Actually, I think the issue is different. For the generalizacion refinement, the sentence is generated in the CHILD OPD (desplegado.opdId), not the root OPD. My test uses `generarOplInteractivo(modelo, desplegado.opdId)` for the "es un" check. Let me verify that the refinement sentence is generated for the child OPD.

Looking at `generarOplInteractivo`: it iterates `opd.apariencias`. For the child OPD (`desplegado.opdId`), the apariencias include `Vehiculo` (contorno) and `Auto`. `Vehiculo` has `refinamiento`, so `oracionRefinamiento` is called. But wait, `oracionRefinamiento` checks `if (!entidad.refinamiento) return null` - Vehiculo does have refinamiento. Then it checks for plegado parcial (no). Then it gets the opdHijo, which is `entidad.refinamiento.opdId`. But wait, that's `desplegado.opdId` itself (the child OPD IS the refinement OPD for Vehiculo). And `aparienciasInternasDeRefinamiento` finds entities inside Vehiculo's contorno in that OPD. 

Hmm, but `aparienciasInternasDeRefinamiento` finds the contorno (Vehiculo's apariencia) and then checks all other apariencias that are WITHIN Vehiculo's contorno. In the child OPD, Vehiculo is at (200, 120) with dimensions 135x60, so its contorno is x:200-335, y:120-180. The child entity `Auto` is at (90, 230) - 90 < 200, so it's NOT within Vehiculo's contorno. Same problem as before!

So the refinement sentence doesn't include Auto because it's outside Vehiculo's bounding box. The `dentroDe` check fails.

I need to fix the coordinates in the test. Let me place children INSIDE the parent entity.

3. **Test #3**: Expected >= 3 nombre tokens but got 2. The aggregation bus merges the 3 enlaces into one sentence. But the tokens only have 2 nombre tokens because in the bus case, the `hintsEnlace` function generates hints for the individual enlace, not for the bus. When there's no abanico, each enlace gets its own sentence, and each sentence has only 2 nombre tokens (origen + destino).

Actually wait, I bet the issue is that `crearEnlace` with `"agregacion"` type triggers the automatic abanico formation in a way I didn't expect. Let me look at `crearEnlace` in operaciones.ts...

Actually, `crearEnlace` in operaciones.ts doesn't call `formarAbanicoAutomatico`. Only the store's action does. But the test calls `crearEnlace` directly, not through the store.

Hmm, but let me look at the test more carefully. The error is at line 851: `generarOplInteractivo(modelo, modelo.opdRaizId)`. If `modelo.opds` is undefined or doesn't have `opdRaizId`, that's the error. Let me check if the model got corrupted.

Actually, I bet the issue is that my test code from earlier test (#3) somehow corrupted the model and that leaked into test #4. But Bun runs tests in isolation per describe block, so that shouldn't happen.

OR, maybe the issue is that when I call `crearEnlace` with agregacion type and the source is an object and the destination is also an object, the bus aggregation logic might interact unexpectedly. But `crearEnlace` in operaciones doesn't do bus aggregation.

1. For HU-50.015 verb token: The issue is that `hintsRefinamiento` generates a verb hint, but the tokenizer might not be matching it. The tokenizer processes hints in order sorted by start position then text length (longest first). If `"**Auto**"` (8 chars) starts at position 0 and `"es un"` (5 chars) starts at position 9, they shouldn't conflict.

Wait, let me check the actual sentence. The `oracionDespliegue` for generalizacion generates:
```
${destino} es un ${nombreOpl(entidad)}.
```
Where destino is `nombreOpl(auto)` = `**Auto**` (if it's an object) and `nombreOpl(vehiculo)` = `**Vehiculo**`.

So the sentence is: `**Auto** es un **Vehiculo**.`

And the hints are:
1. `hintEntidad(vehiculo)` → text: `"**Vehiculo**"`, ref: entidad, rol: "nombre", markdown: "objeto"
2. Hint via verboDespliegue → text: `"es un"`, ref: enlace, rol: "verbo" (if there's an enlace to reference)
3. For each child: hints with enlace ref

Wait, but in my `hintsRefinamiento` code, the hints order is:
1. `hintEntidad(entidad)` for the parent
2. Verb hint
3. For each child: enlace-ref hint

But the SENTENCE starts with `**Auto**`, not `**Vehiculo**`. So the first token should be `**Auto**` which comes from the child hint, not the parent hint.

Actually, looking more carefully at `hintsRefinamiento`, I add:
```ts
const hints: OplTokenHint[] = [hintEntidad(entidad)];  // parent
// ... verb hint
// ... child hints
```

But the tokenizer processes hints in order of their position in the text. The parent hint `hintEntidad(vehiculo)` has text `"**Vehiculo**"` which appears at the END of the sentence. The child hints come later in the hints array but would appear earlier in the text.

The tokenizer in `tokenizarConHints` works by:
1. Flattening all hints with their positions
2. Sorting by start position (priority 1), then by text length descending (priority 2), then by hintIndex (priority 3)
3. Processing sequentially, skipping overlaps

So for the sentence `**Auto** es un **Vehiculo**.`:
- `**Auto**` at pos 0 (child hint) - start 0, end 8
- `es un` at pos 9 (verb hint) - start 9, end 14
- `**Vehiculo**` at pos 15 (parent hint) - start 15, end 27

Since they don't overlap, all three should be found. Let me examine whether the child hint is actually being generated with the correct text.

Looking at the child hint code in my `hintsRefinamiento`:
```ts
hints.push({
  texto: nombreOpl(entidadInterna),
  ref: refEnlace(enlaceHijo.id),
  rol: "nombre",
  markdown: entidadInterna.tipo === "objeto" ? "objeto" : "proceso",
});
```

`nombreOpl(entidadInterna)` for an object returns `**Auto**`. So the tokenizer should find it.

    ...

Where `entidad.id` is Vehiculo's ID. The enlace connects Vehiculo (origen) to Auto (destino). Then for the child hint, `enlaceHijo = enlaceHijoPorEntidadId.get(interna.entidadId)` should return the enlace.

export function crearEstadosIniciales(modelo: Modelo, entidadId: Id): Resultado<EstadosInicialesObjeto> {
  const entidad = modelo.entidades[entidadId];
  if (!entidad) return fallo(`Entidad no existe: ${entidadId}`);
  if (entidad.tipo !== "objeto") return fallo("Los estados sólo aplican a objetos");

  const existentes = estadosDeEntidad(modelo, entidadId);
  if (existentes.length > 0) {
    if (existentes.length === 1) return fallo("Un objeto con estados debe tener al menos dos estados");
    const primero = existentes[0]?.id;
    const segundo = existentes[1]?.id;
    if (!primero || !segundo) return fallo("El objeto tiene estados inválidos");
    return ok({ modelo, estadoIds: [primero, segundo], creado: false });
  }

  const estado1Id = siguienteId(modelo, "s");
  const estado2Id = siguienteId({ ...modelo, nextSeq: modelo.nextSeq + 1 }, "s");
  const estado1: Estado = { id: estado1Id, entidadId, nombre: "estado1" };
  const estado2: Estado = { id: estado2Id, entidadId, nombre: "estado2" };

  return ok({
    modelo: {
      ...modelo,
      nextSeq: modelo.nextSeq + 2,
      estados: {
        ...(modelo.estados ?? {}),
        [estado1Id]: estado1,
        [estado2Id]: estado2,
      },
    },
    estadoIds: [estado1Id, estado2Id],
    creado: true,

```

_Thinking:_

The signature is: `crearEnlace(modelo, opdId, origenId, destinoId, tipo, etiqueta?)`. So `tipo` is the 5th argument, not the 3rd! My test used `crearEnlace(modelo, opdId, "agregacion", objAId, objBId)` which means `origenId = "agregacion"` and `destinoId = objAId` and `tipo = objBId`. This is wrong.

_Thinking:_

3 failures:

1. **editarEtiquetaEnlaceDesdeOpl**: The enlace was not created because `elegirTipoEnlace` → `seleccionarEntidad` doesn't create an enlace in the store. Looking at the store logic, `elegirTipoEnlace` set `modoEnlace.tipo` and `modoEnlace.origenId`. Then clicking on another entity should create the enlace. But maybe the second `seleccionarEntidad` doesn't trigger enlace creation because `modoEnlace` is being reset. Let me check what the store does...

Actually, looking at the store `seleccionarEntidad` function, when `modoEnlace` is active, it should create an enlace. But the flow might be: `seleccionarEntidad(objId)` → sets seleccionId, then `elegirTipoEnlace("agregacion")` → sets modoEnlace, then `seleccionarEntidad(procesoId)` → should create enlace. Let me look at `seleccionarEntidad` in the store...

Actually, the issue might be that `seleccionarEntidad` does NOT create the enlace. Instead, the canvas click handler creates enlaces. The store `seleccionarEntidad` only selects the entity. The user needs to click on an entity on the canvas to create an enlace.

Let me use a different approach for these tests - use `crearEnlace` directly on the model and then call the store action.

2. **exportarOplActualHtml**: `document is not defined` because Bun tests don't have a DOM. I need to mock document.createElement and other DOM APIs in the store test.

_Thinking:_

Several issues:

1. **editarEtiquetaEnlaceDesdeOpl**: The enlace wasn't found after import. The import likely changed the enlace IDs. When using `importarJson`, it calls `hidratarModelo` which generates new IDs via `siguienteId`. So the enlace ID from the original model no longer matches the imported model. I need to find the enlace AFTER importing, not before.

2. **renombrarEstadoDesdeOpl**: Same issue - estado IDs change after import.

3. **abrirInspectorEnlaceDesdeOpl**: Same ID mismatch.

4. **copiarOplActualAlPortapapeles**: `navigator` mock might not be working. Let me check.

5. **exportarOplActualHtml**: `document` mock or OPL generation failing.

Let me fix the first 3 by finding IDs after import, and debug the last 2.

For the first 3 tests, the models created with `crearObjeto`, `crearEnlace`, etc., have specific IDs. After `importarJson(JSON.stringify(exportarModelo(modelo)))`, the `hidratarModelo` function regenerates IDs. So the old enlace IDs don't match the new model. I need to find the enlace in the imported model.

  importarJson(json) {
    const resultado = hidratarModelo(json);
    if (!resultado.ok) {
      set({ mensaje: resultado.error });
      return;
    }
    resetHistorial(resultado.value);
    set(estadoModelo(resultado.value, {
      opdActivoId: resultado.value.opdRaizId,
      seleccionId: null,
      enlaceSeleccionId: null,
      modoEnlace: null,
      modoCreacion: null,
      modeloPersistidoId: null,
      descripcionModeloLocal: "",
      workspaceLocal: workspaceDesdeModelo(resultado.value, null),

```

## Assistant (Steipete · DeepSeek V4 Pro · 94.3s)

_Thinking:_

`importarJson` uses `resetHistorial` and `estadoModelo`. `estadoModelo` returns just the model + extra fields. The `modelo` state is set via `set(estadoModelo(...))`. This should work.

But wait, there's a `beforeEach` that also calls `importarJson(exportarModelo(crearModelo()))`. This might be interfering. The `beforeEach` creates a fresh empty model and imports it, but then each test also calls `importarJson`. Let me check if the second `importarJson` correctly overrides the first.

Then `crearEnlace(modelo, modelo.opdRaizId, ...)` creates the enlace in the same OPD. And `exportarModelo` serializes it. And `hidratarModelo` deserializes it. The enlace should be there.

### Verificación

```
cd app
bun run test    → 404 pass, 0 fail (1991 expect(), 25 archivos)
bun run build   → OK, bundle 915 KB minificado, 261 KB gzip
```

### Decisiones tomadas (documentadas en commits)

1. **Verbo de refinamiento**: `hintsRefinamiento` emite hint de verbo con ref al primer enlace hijo conectado al padre. Para plural (ej. "son"), el verbo se mantiene como texto sin ref de enlace; las oraciones de enlace individual sí tienen token verbo con ref.
2. **Barra de búsqueda y botones**: viven en una sola toolbar superior (fila única con wrap). Sin atajos de teclado (Ctrl+F es de L4 para "Buscar cosas del modelo").
3. **Token multi-enlace**: subrayado punteado (`border-bottom: 1px dotted #93a3b8`) para distinguir tokens con ref de enlace.
4. **Indentación**: cableada a 0 para OPD único activo; el cálculo de profundidad queda listo para HU-50.027.
5. **`aplicarEdicionOpl`**: retorna `Resultado<Modelo>` puro; el store invoca `commitModelo` para integrar undo/redo.

### No tocado
- `docs/HANDOFF.md` — intacto
- `docs/historias-usuario-v2/` — intacto
- Archivos fuera del scope (Toolbar, Serializacion, ArbolOpd, Mapas, Dialogos, MenuPrincipal, CreacionWizard, etc.)

### Bloqueos
- Ninguno. Sin cascadas cross-line detectadas.
- Los tests de store para `editarEtiquetaEnlaceDesdeOpl` con import/export usan atajos (IDs post-import) porque el roundtrip JSON regenera IDs. Cobertura completa en tests unitarios de `edicionCanvas.test.ts`.
